These receptors bind to steroid hormones, thyroid hormone, retinoids and vitamin D among others, dimerize and bind to DNA. Its ligands include testosterone, dehydroepiandrosterone and androstenedione. Stimulation of the receptor activates the SMAD signaling module.\n\nSource: http://www.netpath.org/pathways?path_id=NetPath_4</Comment>\n  <Comment Source=\"WikiPathways-category\">Cellular
